  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_25259657-69ed-420e-82b7-438bb52b5bc3'
      });
    }

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer15690059327891756219">Sebuah upacara gondang mengubah segalanya bagi Alfa. Makhluk misterius yang disebut Si Jaga Portibi tiba-tiba muncul menghantuinya.   <span id="freeText15690059327891756219" style="display:none">Sebuah upacara gondang mengubah segalanya bagi Alfa. Makhluk misterius yang disebut Si Jaga Portibi tiba-tiba muncul menghantuinya. Orang-orang sakti berebut menginginkan Alfa menjadi murid mereka. Dan, yang paling mengerikan dari itu semua adalah setiap tidurnya menjadi pertaruhan nyawa. Sesuatu menunggu Alfa di alam mimpi.<br /><br />Perantauan Alfa jauh membawanya hingga ke Amerika Serikat. Ia berjuang sebagai imigran gelap yang ingin mengubah nasib dan status. Pada suatu malam, kehadiran seseorang memicu Alfa untuk menghadapi ketakutan terbesarnya. Alam mimpinya ternyata menyimpan rahasia besar yang tidak pernah ia bayangkan. Di Lembah Yarlung, Tibet, jawaban mulai terkuak.<br /><br />Sementara itu, pencarian Gio di Rio Tambopata menemui jalan buntu. Pada saat yang tak terduga, pria yang pernah menemuinya di Vallegrande kembali muncul. Pria itu mengarahkan Gio ke pencarian baru. Petunjuknya adalah empat batu bersimbol, merepresentasikan empat orang, dan Gio ternyata adalah salah seorang dari mereka.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15690059327891756219" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>

    <div class="section firstReview">
      

<div id="review_1086530820" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1086530820" />
    <a title="Randy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3859570-randy"><img alt="Randy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1557892584p2/3859570.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1086530820?book_show_action=true">Oct 22, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Randy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Randy" href="/user/show/3859570-randy">Randy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3859570-randy?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3859570-randy?shelf=literary">literary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3859570-randy?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3859570-randy?shelf=indonesian">indonesian</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1086530820" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12019231786765192546"><blockquote><i>"Every night we participate in the most profound mysteries, moving from one dimension experience to another, losing our sense of self and finding it again, and yet we take it for granted."</i> <b>-Tenzin Wangyal Rinpoche</b></blockquote><br/><br/>Years ago after I finished reading Petir and found out that the fifth instalment would be titled as "Gelombang" with Alfa as the main character, there was this big curiosity in my mind; about what the book would be all about and how the character would be. I thought Gelombang would be a</span>
  <span id="freeText12019231786765192546" style="display:none"><blockquote><i>"Every night we participate in the most profound mysteries, moving from one dimension experience to another, losing our sense of self and finding it again, and yet we take it for granted."</i> <b>-Tenzin Wangyal Rinpoche</b></blockquote><br /><br />Years ago after I finished reading Petir and found out that the fifth instalment would be titled as "Gelombang" with Alfa as the main character, there was this big curiosity in my mind; about what the book would be all about and how the character would be. I thought Gelombang would be about time-space experience and Alfa would be a physic geek. But, surprise, surprise... It's more about the spiritual metaphor of Gelombang. The book is about Dream: one of the most mysterious dimension ever exist in the matrix of universe. It's no coincidence that the book is about one of the things I've always been fascinated about. Ever since I was a child I've had my own experiences with dreams, a lot of them are fictional with real story plot and some of them are symbolic, fantastical, and feel almost sacred. Even once or twice I've even experienced a lucid dream for a very short moment.<br /><br />This spiritual yet also scientific topic is what I adore the most, thanks to Dewi Lester to that. I feel so nostalgic and so close about this book because Alfa's life journey reminds me of my mother. They both come from a very remote area, moved to the big city, and finally reached the centre new world: United States. They both struggled very hard to survive and to get on with life. Beside the background places which took place in New York and also Tibet, what I like more about this book is the story has more actions to it, the first after the second instalment, Akar. We didn't get Elektra and Zarah to face grave danger in Petir and Partikel, respectively.<br /><br />And finally, I feel like the plot twists about:<br />-the symbolic stones, which appear to be 6 not only 4: meaning there are actually 6 Avatars<br />-Asko<br />-the Harbinger, the Infiltrant, and the Sarvara<br />-Bintang Jatuh (The Falling Star)<br />-Ishtar Summer<br />-Kell<br />-(and basically about the whole details in this Supernova saga)<br />...has blown my mind. I can not be saved.<br /><br />I just don't have the right words to express this abundance feelings I am and have always been having towards this creation of Dewi Lestari's. She is like this human yet not too human, possibly coming from other dimension, or possibly a human vessel to the very old wise and amazing soul coming from other entity that is different from our world. She is like a saviour. She is a Supernova. She has given me a chance to be a part of this amazing journey. Sadly, we all are only one instalment away from the end of this amazing, mind-blowing, spiritually heart-shaking, journey.<br /><br />Supernova: 2001-2014.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12019231786765192546" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

Anyway, applause for Dee's in depth research on Batak cosmology, dream walker, and every place that serves as setting in this book. This proves her as one of the best writer in our Nation. <div id="review_1082206309" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1082206309" />
    <a title="Juliana" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15022196-juliana"><img alt="Juliana" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1520433920p2/15022196.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1082206309?book_show_action=true">Oct 16, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Juliana" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Juliana" href="/user/show/15022196-juliana">Juliana</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15022196-juliana?shelf=novel">novel</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1082206309" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12419226718234972200">got this book yesterday, one day ahead of the born day, which is today.<br/>read this book for almost 8 hours, finished by almost 3a.m<br/><br/>as always, i love supernova series as they never disappointed me, or should i say that the writer, Dee, never did. The first 15 pages reminded me of the first episode of Supernova, and the remaining one reminded me of every character that has made the journey so far. Everyone from the first till now, and i hope when i write this review, i don't give you all the spoiler</span>
  <span id="freeText12419226718234972200" style="display:none">got this book yesterday, one day ahead of the born day, which is today.<br />read this book for almost 8 hours, finished by almost 3a.m<br /><br />as always, i love supernova series as they never disappointed me, or should i say that the writer, Dee, never did. The first 15 pages reminded me of the first episode of Supernova, and the remaining one reminded me of every character that has made the journey so far. Everyone from the first till now, and i hope when i write this review, i don't give you all the spoiler. but i can't help if by any chance, i must say it, so be aware. :D<br /><br />why i write in english? i think this is the after effect from getting carried away by Alfa and his journey till New York that almost entire conversation was done in English. hahaha<br /><br />Well, mari bersua dengan bahasa nasional kita. Sekali lagi, Dewi Lestari menciptakan Alfa dan membawaku ikut bertualang dengannya. Hal yang selalu aku kagumi dari tulisannya, halaman pertama menciptakan gerbang masuk yang kemudian di dalamnya aku berkenalan dengan tokoh utama dari buku tersebut. Aku mengakui bahwa, tulisan di dalam serial supernova, terkadang sulit dipahami, terkadang perlu membaca satu kalimat berulang-kali, but who cares? as long as i still got carried away in the end, by the Alfa, hisself.<br /><br />I dont know why, hampir setiap kalimat yang dipilih membuat bulu kuduk berdiri saat membacanya, mungkin karena lingkungan Alfa yang berbicara dengan gaib, atau karena petualangannya yang terlalu luar biasa. Diksi dari cerita Dee selalu menarik, menarik dalam arti sebenarnya, dan "menarik" pembacanya hanyut, diterjang gelombang, dan aku salah satunya.<br /><br />i have always wondered, what will be the end of this story? since i still try to connect the dot every here and there, every now and then, and i still haven't thought of anything. Pencerahan sih setelah petualangan Alfa ini, setidaknya sebuah rencana tersampaikan, meskipun aku belum tau apa itu, tapi mendengar Alfa mengingat rencananya, sepertinya terlalu besar dan rumit, atau mungkin terlalu sederhana. Entahlah, aku berhenti berusaha menebak, menikmati arus cerita, berencana membaca ulang semuanya dan menunggu lagi "Intelegensi Embun Pagi".<br /><br />I am happy that Dee always find something to tell, from the things i don't even know it exist, till things that i have always been curious about it, something like "lucid dream" makes me like "Gelombang" even more, membuat Gelombang memiliki tambahan nilai tambah yang memang sudah ada meskipun dia tidak membahasnya. It's just personal interest, though. Dan tambahan bahasa asingnya, well, i learned a lot from Alfa and waiting for more to happen in the next series, dan bertanya2 itukah yang terakhir?<br /><br />i wrote this in my blog also, feel free to visit, maybe? hehehe<br />somewhatserendipity.blogspot.com</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Zahrina Mardina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Zahrina Mardina" href="/user/show/17428117-zahrina-mardina">Zahrina Mardina</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer2517773388623223262">I just want to make a fair judgement. Well i read some negative comments. but i have to confess Dee gave a good hard work. We can see from the details she gave, it can be clearly seen that info cant be leaked out easily. I was amazed by the Oneironautics details. it is not easy to handle and she proved that she is incredibly smart and passionate!<br/>and about 'unnecessary figures' that people said such as Nicky, i just want to say, we still have one more "intelegensi embun pagi" can't you try for be</span>
  <span id="freeText2517773388623223262" style="display:none">I just want to make a fair judgement. Well i read some negative comments. but i have to confess Dee gave a good hard work. We can see from the details she gave, it can be clearly seen that info cant be leaked out easily. I was amazed by the Oneironautics details. it is not easy to handle and she proved that she is incredibly smart and passionate!<br />and about 'unnecessary figures' that people said such as Nicky, i just want to say, we still have one more "intelegensi embun pagi" can't you try for being a bit patient and just see what happen with them?<br /> <br />I see Supernova as the accumulation of patience to build a complete puzzle. Dee completes the puzzle fragment by fragment. Not all of the writer have this ability. She knows from the beginning about what she want to do. She offers 'differences' that we should respect. She brings the social critics that figured out our society, that differences still cant be accepted very well in our society. for me, the way she tell this is worthy. Even though until the end, i still did'nt get what is actually that 'team' purpose. what is the mission? how important is the mission that it can make so many people include themselves to help that team? yeap it looks like i have to wait for the latest book to be able to understand. <br /><br />But still, i know it is subjective, but i still love 'Akar' and 'Petir' more than Partikel and Gelombang. I cant remember the detail in Partikel but i clearly remember the details in petir and akar even though i just read them once. I know i shouldnt say it but too many mystical things no matter it can be related with science it disturbs me. somehow what happened with Bodhi and Elektra sounds more acceptable and realistic. <br /><br />Finally, thanks for the amazing gift Dee. you still did good. i am waiting for the last puzzle fragment. I hope it will answer all of my curiosity. Best of luck! </span>

<div id="review_1088013411" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1088013411" />
    <a title="Frilla Amanda" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30335915-frilla-amanda"><img alt="Frilla Amanda" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1424020894p2/30335915.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1088013411?book_show_action=true">Oct 24, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Frilla Amanda" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Frilla Amanda" href="/user/show/30335915-frilla-amanda">Frilla Amanda</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1088013411" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11855240427951844480">It was a wild ride. I actually quite fond of Alfa and how he's grown from a geek child into a dashing, genius workaholic (still a geek, I suppose, a handsome one though). The plot itself was enjoyable, although a bit tad boring for me. It's kinda predictable. But since this is the 5th book and the author is trying to connect the dots between the books, I suppose it's okay.<br/><br/>The humor though... Thomas Alfa Edison, Albert Einstein and Sir Isaac Newton. It's so pitiful and funny at the same time. I a</span>
  <span id="freeText11855240427951844480" style="display:none">It was a wild ride. I actually quite fond of Alfa and how he's grown from a geek child into a dashing, genius workaholic (still a geek, I suppose, a handsome one though). The plot itself was enjoyable, although a bit tad boring for me. It's kinda predictable. But since this is the 5th book and the author is trying to connect the dots between the books, I suppose it's okay.<br /><br />The humor though... Thomas Alfa Edison, Albert Einstein and Sir Isaac Newton. It's so pitiful and funny at the same time. I also fond of how the tough Rodrigo was actually a sucker for telenovela. Lol. And of course the friendship between Alfa, Troy and Carlo. I like the dynamic between them, I think they deserve their own story. A story about their friendship through high school and university... I'll definitely dig that.<br /><br />All in all, I think the characterization in this book beats the other books in Supernova series. <br /><br />(One thing that bother me was how the korean gangster used formal speech with Alfa, it just doesn't make sense for him to give much respect to a kid.)</span>
  <a data-text-id="11855240427951844480" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer4991514449355406842">Home.<br/><br/>That's exactly what I felt when I was reading this. The setting (North Sumatra) and the language (Bahasa Indonesia Medan) cured my homesickness a bit.<br/><br/>However, the storyline itself is not as mind-blowing as I expected. True that Dee is a good writer and she describes things very well, but this is one draggy novel. Some parts are "Kok gampang banget sih sepertinya?" While the other parts are "Buset, dibikin susah banget!" I agree with some other reviews that stated this novel is such a best-s</span>
  <span id="freeText4991514449355406842" style="display:none">Home.<br /><br />That's exactly what I felt when I was reading this. The setting (North Sumatra) and the language (Bahasa Indonesia Medan) cured my homesickness a bit.<br /><br />However, the storyline itself is not as mind-blowing as I expected. True that Dee is a good writer and she describes things very well, but this is one draggy novel. Some parts are "Kok gampang banget sih sepertinya?" While the other parts are "Buset, dibikin susah banget!" I agree with some other reviews that stated this novel is such a best-seller because of the brand, not the story. This is supposed to be the last book before the finale, yet I am still clueless about where the story is heading. Will there be a war? What is the war about? What is so dangerous about the both worlds?<br /><br />Although I am a bit disappointed in this novel, I am looking forward to Intelejensi Embun Pagi. I need answers to my questions. <br /><br /></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('zawh+e1h58IOerH839H0r9oJMPcHguM/pxi6WWSFOP3bPWs9rz2aQYiErhUde7HwxPpbdDZY4p/sNuvFH0gKNw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('5Pk1+ikE739ER4+SUaorh3M21Gm1hPB6i8P7WkYlQwnyaH8+a1iS/MK5kHuTAG7YbcW/6oRe8drA7arGPehxww==')})
  }

Bersama kawan-kawannya, Daniel Tumbuan, Sunu Dyantoro, Alex Perazon, dia dibawa ke sebuah tempat yang tak dikenal. Berbulan-bulan mereka disekap, diinterogasi, dipukul, ditendang, digantung, dan disetrum agar bersedia menjawab satu pertanyaan penting: siapakah yang berdiri di balik gerakan aktivis dan mahasiswa saat itu.\n\nJakarta, Juni 1998\n\nKeluarga Arya Wibisono, seperti biasa, pada hari Minggu sore memasak bersama, menyediakan makanan kesukaan Biru Laut. Sang ayah akan meletakkan satu piring untuk dirinya, satu piring untuk sang ibu, satu piring untuk Biru Laut, dan satu piring untuk si bungsu Asmara Jati. Mereka duduk menanti dan menanti. Tapi Biru Laut tak kunjung muncul.\n\nJakarta, 2000\n\nAsmara Jati, adik Biru Laut, beserta Tim Komisi Orang Hilang yang dipimpin Aswin Pradana mencoba mencari jejak mereka yang hilang serta merekam dan mempelajari testimoni mereka yang kembali. Anjani, kekasih Laut, para orangtua dan istri aktivis yang hilang menuntut kejelasan tentang anggota keluarga mereka. Sementara Biru Laut, dari dasar laut yang sunyi bercerita kepada kita, kepada dunia tentang apa yang terjadi pada dirinya dan kawan-kawannya.\n\nLaut Bercerita, novel terbaru Leila S. Chudori, bertutur tentang kisah keluarga yang kehilangan, sekumpulan sahabat yang merasakan kekosongan di dada, sekelompok orang yang gemar menyiksa dan lancar berkhianat, sejumlah keluarga yang <div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer2223179481623599088">Dee Lestari, is one of the bestselling and critically acclaimed writers in Indonesia.<br/>Born in January 20, 1976, she began her debut with a serial novel: Supernova in 2001. Supernova’s first episode, <i>Kesatria, Putri, dan Bintang Jatuh</i> (The Knight, The Princess, and The Falling Star), was sold phenomenally, achieving a cult status among Indonesian young readers. She has published four other episodes:</span>
  <span id="freeText2223179481623599088" style="display:none">Dee Lestari, is one of the bestselling and critically acclaimed writers in Indonesia.<br />Born in January 20, 1976, she began her debut with a serial novel: Supernova in 2001. Supernova’s first episode, <i>Kesatria, Putri, dan Bintang Jatuh</i> (The Knight, The Princess, and The Falling Star), was sold phenomenally, achieving a cult status among Indonesian young readers. She has published four other episodes: <i>Akar</i> (The Root), <i>Petir</i> (The Lightning), <i>Partikel</i>(The Particle), and <i>Gelombang</i> (The Wave). <br />Aside of the Supernova series, Dee has also published a novel titled <i>Perahu Kertas</i> (Paper Boat), and three anthologies: <i>Filosofi Kopi</i> (Coffee’s Philosophy), <i>Madre</i>, and <i>Rectoverso</i> — a unique hybrid of music and literature. <br />Dee also has an extensive music career, producing four albums with her former vocal trio, and two solo albums. She has been writing songs for renowned Indonesian artists. <br /><i>Perahu Kertas</i> (Paper Boat) was turned into a movie in 2009, marking Dee’s debut as a screenplay writer. The movie became one of the national's block busters. Following the same path, <i>Madre, Filosofi Kopi, Madre,</i> and <i>Supernova KPBJ,</i> were made into movies. <br />In February 2016, Dee released the final episode of Supernova, <i>Inteligensi Embun Pagi</i> (Intelligence of the Morning Dew). All Dee’s books are published by Bentang Pustaka. </span>
  <a data-text-id="2223179481623599088" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>

<script>
//<![CDATA[
      var newTip = new Tip($('bookCover_1300350'), "\n\n  <h2><a class=\"readable bookTitle\" href=\"https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1300350.Supernova?from_choice=false&amp;from_home_module=false\">Supernova: Akar<\/a><\/h2>\n\n      <div>\n        by <a class=\"authorName\" href=\"/author/show/164478.Dee_Lestari?origin=series_works\">Dee Lestari<\/a><span title=\"Goodreads Author!\">*<\/span>\n      <\/div>\n\n          <div class=\"smallText uitext darkGreyText\">\n            <span class=\"minirating\"><span class=\"stars staticStars notranslate\"><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p6\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p0\"><\/span><\/span> 3.83 avg rating &mdash; 9,425 ratings<\/span>            &mdash; published 2002\n          <\/div>\n\n    <div class=\"addBookTipDescription\">\n      \n<span id=\"freeTextContainer4754154642876510257\">Talita Luna\nKesejatian hidup ada pada batu kerikil yang tertendang ketika kau melangkah\nmenyusuri jalan. Kesejatian hidup ada pada selembar daun kering yang gugur\ntertiup angin. Kesejatian hidup ada air susu ibu yang yang merelakan puting\npayudaranya<\/span>\n  <span id=\"freeText4754154642876510257\" style=\"display:none\">Talita Luna\nKesejatian hidup ada pada batu kerikil yang tertendang ketika kau melangkah\nmenyusuri jalan. Kesejatian hidup ada pada selembar daun kering yang gugur\ntertiup angin. Kesejatian hidup ada air susu ibu yang yang merelakan puting\npayudaranya diisap oleh bayi manapun. Di\nVihara Pit Yong Kiong, Pasuruan, di pelabuhan Belawan, di Penang, di\nBangkok, di Laos, di Golden Triangle, di Cambodia, di Bandung, di\nmanapun kau hidup.\n\nTapi, dia mungkin tak terlihat pada arus politik yang menyudutkanmu pada\npilihan kedigdayaan. Dia menyembunyikan diri dari teriakan-\nteriakan yang menggemakan perubahan. Kesejatian hidup tak memerlukan\nperubahan, namun juga tak menampiknya. Dia rebah pada semua kesederhanaan\nyang ada di sekelilingmu. Maka, carilah, dan kamu akan mendapatinya.\nKetuklah, maka pintu akan dibukakan bagimu. Mintalah, maka kau akan diberi.\n\nDemikianlah Dewi Lestari mewakilkan sebuah upaya pencarian kesejatian hidup\npada seorang tokoh bernama Bodhi. Seorang bayi yang di suatu pagi tergeletak\ndi pintu Vihara. Dipungut, diasuh, dan dididik oleh seorang Pandita, Guru\nLiong. Merasa bahwa karma pada hidup masa lalunya sangat berat. 18 tahun\ndididik dengan ketat, termasuk penguasaan terhadap sebuah ilmu bela diri,\nBodhi mengalami penyempurnaan bathin. Pemurnian spirit. Termasuk sejumlah\npengalaman uniknya yang &quot;merasa&quot; menjadi ulat, tikus got, kucing, dan sapi.\n\n18 tahun adalah waktu yang cukup, dan Bodhi mohon pamit. Bersama serombongan\npendeta Buddha, Bodhi menyeberang ke Sumatera dan memutuskan menetap di\ndaerah Belawan. Tanpa KTP, tak juga faham mengenai asal usul dan tanggal\nkelahirannya. Bekerja tiga bulan, mendapat upah, dan dibantu oleh Ompu\nBerlin untuk mendapatkan sejumlah dokumen identitas termasuk paspor, Bodhi\nmenyeberang ke Penang. Disana dia bertemu dengan sejumlah backpackers yang\nkemudian &quot;memberi&quot; arah perjalanan berikutnya: Bangkok.\n\nBangkok surga bagi para backpackers. Ratusan pengelana dari mancanegara\ntumpah di sana. Bodhi tinggal di semua rumah penginapan Srinthip bersama\nsejumlah backpakers multi etnis. Penghuninya datang dan pergi. Masuklah\nKell, seorang lelaki tampan, peranakan Irlandia dan Mesir. Lelaki tertampan\nyang mungkin pernah ada di bumi ini yang mempunyai tugas kehidupan untuk\nmembubuhkan 617 tatto pada 617 orang untuk membuat dirinya menyongsong\nkemerdekaan paripurna setelah orang ke-617 membubuhkan tato yang ke-618 ke\ntubuhnya. Lelaki yang kerap menyenandungkan Eye in The Sky-nya Alan Parson\nProject. Kell kemudian mengajarinya tattoo. Lalu, jadilah Bodhi seorang\ntattooist dan menjadikan itu sebagai cara untuk mendapatkan uang bagi biaya\nhidup sehari-hari.\n\nSeorang backpacker perempuan bernama Star, berasal dari Hollywood, peranakan\nEropa Timur dan Timur Tengah masuk dan menginap di Srinthip. Perempuan\ncantik dan tercantik yang pernah dilihat Bodhi. Perawakan tubuhnya sempurna.\nPerempuan inilah yang memperkenalkan dirinya dengan sebuah perasaan lain\nyang belum pernah dia rasakan sepanjang hidup. Star minta Bodhi mentattoonya\ntepat di payudara.Dan bergetarlah kulit semesta. Bergerolalah gelombang\nsamudera. Erangan kesakitan Star sewaktu ditattoo adalah hasrat dedaunan\nyang mendambakan sapuan sinar matahari. Waktu berlalu dan mereka berpisah.\nEntah kenapa.\n\nBodhi meneruskan pencarian kesejatiannya. Star seolah menggenap kesempurnaan\ntattoonya dan pergi menyongsong kelana berikut.\nKeterserakan yang tak menyenangkan. Tapi hidup adalah keping-keping misteri\nyang baru terbuka setelah rebah sepenuhnya. Bodhi membiarkan semesta\nmenuntun perjalanan selanjutnya. Bertemu dengan lelaki tua pengasuh Bob\nMarley, yang mengumandangkan reggae seolah cuma itu yang ada di bumi dan\nkahyangan. Bertemu kembali dengan Tristan, backpacker yang ditemuinya\npertama kali di Penang. Mereka berdua bekerja di ladang ganja di Golden\nTriangle dengan upah USD 700 per minggu. Sekian bulan di sana Bodhi memiliki\ncukup uang untuk melanjutkan kembara berikutnya. Pulang ke Srinthip\ndidapatinya Kell sudah tak ada. Ah, lelaki yang telah memberinya keceriaan\ndan sebuah warna baru.\n\nRasa kangennya memuncak. Diputuskannya untuk pergi mencari Kell. Tak ada\npetunjuk. Tak ada berita. Dan dia pergi. Suara semesta dan kerinduannya\nadalah dua buah kompas sejati yang dia percaya akan mengantarkannya tepat\nwaktu - tepat arah kepada Kell. Bodhi terdampar di sebuah pertarungan antar\nmanusia ala Golden Triangle ditonton oleh ribuan petaruh. Diadu secara\nbarbar di atas ring melawan gladiator raksasa. Pertarungan dahsyat dengan\nmenggunakan sejumlah jurus wushu yang mendebarkan pun digelar.\n\nPerjalanan itu begitu panjang dan melelahkan. Menembus belukar di antara\ndesingan peluru. Menyusuri daratan ranjau. Disana dia betemu Epona, gadis\npenakluk ranjau. Disana pula ia bertemu kembali dengan Kell. Lalu, pada\nsebuah kunjungan ke lokasi ranjau, tattoo ke 618, angka kebebasan paripurna\nKell, dirajahkan. Dalam dialog cerdas, konyol, menggelikan, dan bertabur air\nmata. Adegan mengejutkan, dan merupakan bagian terindah. Kebebasan itu\ndatang dan menyapa dalam damai. Nikmati adegan ini sambil mendengarkan You\nTake My Breath Away-nya QUEEN.
